<body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><br><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Exhibit
99.1</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><img src="acl6k0329durezolex9911.jpg" alt=""></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon
Completes Acquisition of Durezol&#8482; and Zyclorin&#8482; from Sirion</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#8211; March 29, 2010 &#8211; </font><font color="blue" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon</font>
(NYSE: <font color="blue" style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">ACL</font>), the world&#8217;s leader in eye care, announced today that it
received regulatory approval and finalized the acquisition of the rights in the
United States for DUREZOL&#8482; emulsion and the global rights, excluding Latin
America, for ZYCLORIN&#8482; from Sirion Therapeutics, Inc.&#160;&#160;Alcon will
immediately assume all marketing, promotion and sales of
DUREZOL&#8482;.&#160;&#160;Management said that it is continuing to evaluate options
to acquire ZIRGAN&#8482;, an antiviral recently approved by the FDA for the treatment
of acute herpetic keratitis (corneal ulcers).</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>DUREZOL&#8482; emulsion is a topical
ophthalmic corticosteroid used to treat postoperative inflammation and pain
associated with ocular surgery and received approval from the U.S. Food and Drug
Administration (FDA) in 2008.&#160;&#160;Currently under clinical investigation
to treat dry eye and other ocular surface diseases, ZYCLORIN&#8482; is a topical
ophthalmic immunomodulator and immunosuppressive agent.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>&#8220;This acquisition reinforces our
ability to drive growth in the near-term with the acquisition of DUREZOL&#8482; and
add products to our long-term research pipeline with ZYCLORIN&#8482;,&#8221; said Stuart
Raetzman, vice president, Global Marketing and area president for the United
States. &#8220;Durezol&#8217;s unique capability to effectively and quickly treat both
inflammation and pain following ocular surgery makes it a great fit for Alcon&#8217;s
leading product portfolio.&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Ocular Inflammation</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Cataracts
and glaucoma affect more than 24 million people age 40 and older in the United
States.&#160;&#160;Many of these people seek surgical treatment for these and
other eye conditions.&#160;&#160;Corticosteroids and non-steroidal
anti-inflammatory drugs are commonly used after eye surgery to manage
postoperative pain and inflammation.&#160;&#160;Complications can occur if
inflammation is left untreated and can interfere with a patient&#8217;s visual
rehabilitation.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
DUREZOL<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8482;</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">DUREZOL<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8482;</font> (difluprednate ophthalmic
emulsion) 0.05% is a topical ophthalmic corticosteroid for the treatment of
postoperative inflammation and pain associated with ocular
surgery.&#160;&#160;DUREZOL&#8482; received approval from the FDA in 2008 and was the
first ophthalmic steroid to be approved for both postoperative inflammation and
pain.&#160;&#160;Clinical trials demonstrated that DUREZOL&#8482; reduced ocular pain
and inflammation rapidly and effectively for patients following ocular
surgery.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">DUREZOL<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8482;</font> emulsion is a
difluorinated derivative of prednisolone with a recommended dosing regimen of
one drop four times daily beginning 24 hours after surgery and continuing
throughout the first two weeks of the postoperative period, followed by two
times daily for a week and then tapering off thereafter based on the
response.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">-
more -</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
        </div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>The most common ocular adverse
reactions occurring in 5&#8211;15% of subjects in clinical studies with DUREZOL&#8482;
emulsion included corneal edema, ciliary and conjunctival hyperemia, eye pain,
photophobia, posterior capsule opacification, anterior chamber cells, anterior
chamber flare, conjunctival edema and blepharitis.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">About ZYCLORIN</font>&#8482;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ZYCLORIN&#8482;
(cyclosporine) is a topical ophthalmic immunomodulator and immunosuppressive
agent.&#160;&#160;ZYCLORIN&#8482; is an investigational drug and is not approved by
the U.S. Food and Drug Administration.&#160;&#160;It is being studied for the
treatment of ocular surface diseases, including dry eye, which affects millions
of Americans.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Alcon</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon,
Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.5
billion in 2009.&#160;&#160;Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic
industry for 65 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets
pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contacts lens solutions and
other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions
of the eye.&#160;&#160;Alcon operates in 75 countries and sells products in 180
markets.&#160;&#160;For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s web
site at <font color="blue" style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.alcon.com</font>.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"># #
